#  ██████╗ ██████╗ ██╗   ██╗███╗   ██╗████████╗██████╗ ██╗   ██╗     ██████╗██████╗ ███████╗██████╗ ██╗████████╗    ██████╗  █████╗ ████████╗██╗███╗   ██╗ ██████╗
# ██╔════╝██╔═══██╗██║   ██║████╗  ██║╚══██╔══╝██╔══██╗╚██╗ ██╔╝    ██╔════╝██╔══██╗██╔════╝██╔══██╗██║╚══██╔══╝    ██╔══██╗██╔══██╗╚══██╔══╝██║████╗  ██║██╔════╝
# ██║     ██║   ██║██║   ██║██╔██╗ ██║   ██║   ██████╔╝ ╚████╔╝     ██║     ██████╔╝█████╗  ██║  ██║██║   ██║       ██████╔╝███████║   ██║   ██║██╔██╗ ██║██║  ███╗
# ██║     ██║   ██║██║   ██║██║╚██╗██║   ██║   ██╔══██╗  ╚██╔╝      ██║     ██╔══██╗██╔══╝  ██║  ██║██║   ██║       ██╔══██╗██╔══██║   ██║   ██║██║╚██╗██║██║   ██║
# ╚██████╗╚██████╔╝╚██████╔╝██║ ╚████║   ██║   ██║  ██║   ██║       ╚██████╗██║  ██║███████╗██████╔╝██║   ██║       ██║  ██║██║  ██║   ██║   ██║██║ ╚████║╚██████╔╝
#  ╚═════╝ ╚═════╝  ╚═════╝ ╚═╝  ╚═══╝   ╚═╝   ╚═╝  ╚═╝   ╚═╝        ╚═════╝╚═╝  ╚═╝╚══════╝╚═════╝ ╚═╝   ╚═╝       ╚═╝  ╚═╝╚═╝  ╚═╝   ╚═╝   ╚═╝╚═╝  ╚═══╝ ╚═════╝

country_credit_rating = {
	set_variable = {
		name = country_credit_note_fixe
		value = country_credit_pondered_mean
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			#var:country_credit_note_fixe = 10
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 9
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 9
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 8
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_AA
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 8
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 7
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_A
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 7
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 6
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_BBB
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 6
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 5
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_BB
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 5
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 4
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_B
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 4
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 3
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_CCC
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 3
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 2
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 2
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 1
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_C
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			var:country_credit_note_fixe < 1
			var:country_credit_note_fixe >= 0
			not  = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_D
		}
	}

	#clean country_credit_rating
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			or = {
				var:country_bankruptcy = 1
				var:economic_crisis = 1
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				var:financial_crash = 1
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
	}

	#############################################################################
	#exit_from_crisis -> réinitialise les compteur

	#declared_bankruptcy
	if = {
		limit  = {
			#var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			var:country_bankruptcy = 1 #country_bankruptcy & central_bank_bankruptcy n'ont pas d'avertissement il déclanche directement la crise donc ils doivent etre reset automatiquement aprs avoir perdu le modificateur
			not = {
				has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = country_bankruptcy
			value = 0
		}
		economic_instability_count_reset = yes
	}
	#currency_crisis_country
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			var:currency_crisis = 1
			not = {
				has_modifier = currency_crisis_country
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = currency_crisis
			value = 0
		}
		economic_instability_count_reset = yes
	}
	#central_bank_bankruptcy_country
	if = {
		limit  = {
			#var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
			not = {
				has_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = central_bank_bankruptcy
			value = 0
		}
		economic_instability_count_reset = yes
	}
	#financial_crash_country
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			var:financial_crash = 1
			not = {
				has_modifier = financial_crash_country
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = financial_crash
			value = 0
		}
		economic_instability_count_reset = yes
	}
	#economic_crisis_country
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			var:economic_crisis = 1
			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_crisis_country
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = economic_crisis
			value = 0
		}
		economic_instability_count_reset = yes
	}

	############################################################################

	#economic_instability
	# -> attribu les notation en fonction des crise en court
	# -> normalement si un pays sort d'une crise (fin des moddifier) -> les compteur sont réinitialiser avant d'ariver içi
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
			var:country_bankruptcy = 1
			not = {
				var:economic_crisis = 1
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				var:financial_crash = 1
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_C #tant que le  modificateur déclarre  bankrrupsi n'est pas enlevé
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_modifier = economic_instability
			var:economic_crisis = 1
			not = {
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				var:financial_crash = 1
				var:country_bankruptcy = 1
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_modifier = economic_instability
			var:financial_crash = 1
			not = {
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				var:economic_crisis = 1
				var:country_bankruptcy = 1
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit  = { #country_credit_rating_D notation D deja attribué pour 23 mois pas de renotation entre temps
			has_modifier = economic_instability
			or = {
				var:currency_crisis = 1
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
			}
			not = {
				var:financial_crash = 1
				var:economic_crisis = 1
				var:country_bankruptcy = 1
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_D
			months = 12 #à verif lors d'une currency crisisi
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit  = {
			has_modifier = economic_instability
			interconnected_crises > 1
		}
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		add_modifier = {
			name = country_credit_rating_D
			months = 12 #à verif lors d'une currency crisisi
		}
	}

	#economic_instability reset by year if nothing appen in year #probleme car si reset chaque anné peut plus y avoir de crise donc voir pour abaissé de 0.5/an
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			var:economic_crisis = 0
			var:financial_crash = 0
			var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 0
			var:currency_crisis = 0
			#var:country_bankruptcy = 0
			not = {
				has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
				has_modifier = currency_crisis_country
				has_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
				has_modifier = financial_crash_country
				has_modifier = economic_crisis_country
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = economic_instability_count
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
sovereign_bond_yields = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.04 0.05 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.05 0.06 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.06 0.07 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.07 0.08 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.08 0.09 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.09 0.1 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.10 0.11 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.11 0.12 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.12 0.13 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			value = { 0.13 0.15 }
		}
	}

	#test
	else_if = {
		limit  = {
			not = {
				country_credit_rating_national_debt_compared_gdp_malus_100_on_interest_rate = 1
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = target_interest_rate
			multiply = country_credit_rating_national_debt_compared_gdp_malus_100_on_interest_rate
		}
	}
}
economic_instability_count_reset = {
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count >= 2
			var:economic_crisis = 0
			var:financial_crash = 0
			var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 0
			var:currency_crisis = 0
			#var:country_bankruptcy = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = economic_instability_count
			value = 0
		}
		country_credit_rating = yes
	}
}

credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week = {
	remove_modifier = interest_at_the_central_bank
	add_modifier = {
		name = interest_at_the_central_bank
		multiplier = credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_month_by_inflation
	}
}
credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week_off = {
	remove_modifier = interest_at_the_central_bank
}
ai_credit_at_central_bank = {
	if  = {
		limit = { #pays avec tresorerie faible or de la guerre donc strategie d'endettement constant et roulement de la dette
			credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week_by_inflation < part_budget_authorized_debt_interest
			national_debt_compared_gdp < national_debt_allowed_relative_gdp
			gold_reserve_compared_gold_reserves_limit < 0.1
			is_at_war = no
		}
		add_treasury = {
			add = national_debt_allowed_in_gold
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_bond_var_state_1
					add = owner.bond_producted
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = government_loan
			add = national_debt_allowed_in_currency
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = credit_at_central_bank
			add = national_debt_allowed_in_gold
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit  = { #pays en guerre avec reserve inf à 25%, a bessoin d'un coup de mains equivalent la dif pour atteindre 25% + 25% -> pas de limite donc possibilité de faire des 100ain% de dette
			gold_reserve_compared_gold_reserves_limit < 0.15
			is_at_war = yes
		}
		add_treasury = {
			add = national_debt_allowed_in_gold_war
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_bond_var_state_1
					add = owner.bond_producted_war
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = government_loan
			add = national_debt_allowed_in_currency_war
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = credit_at_central_bank
			add = national_debt_allowed_in_gold_war
		}
	}
}
ai_refund_central_bank = {
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			gold_reserves_var > 0
			national_debt_unauthorized < gold_reserves_var
			var:credit_at_central_bank > national_debt_allowed_in_gold
			is_at_war = no
		}
		add_treasury = {
			subtract = national_debt_unauthorized
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = government_loan
			subtract = national_debt_unauthorized
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:government_loan < 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = government_loan
				value = 0
			}
		}

		change_variable = {
			name = credit_at_central_bank
			subtract = national_debt_unauthorized
		}
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week_by_inflation > part_budget_authorized_debt_interest
			national_debt_refund_more_25_at_refund > 0
			is_at_war = no
		}
		# add_treasury = {
		# 	subtract = national_debt_unauthorized #ai_cheat ?
		# }
		change_variable = {
			name = government_loan
			subtract = national_debt_refund_more_25_at_refund
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:government_loan < 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = government_loan
				value = 0
			}
		}

		change_variable = {
			name = credit_at_central_bank
			subtract = national_debt_refund_more_25_at_refund
		}
	}
}

stockpile_finacial_product = {
	stockpiling_bond_1 = yes
	stockpiling_manufacture_stock_1 = yes
	stockpiling_agricultural_stock_1 = yes
	stockpiling_mining_stock_1 = yes
	stockpiling_railroad_stock_1 = yes
}

stockpiling_bond_1 = {
    set_variable = {
        name = stockpiling_bond_var_2
        value = 0
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            bond_market_goods_buy_orders > 0
			stockpiling_bond_var_1 < 1000000
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = stockpiling_bond_var_2
			add = bond_market_goods_buy_orders
			#add = bond_market_goods_delta
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = stockpiling_bond_var_2
            multiply = 4
        }
		stockpiling_bond_2_state = yes
    }
}
stockpiling_bond_2_state = {
    every_scope_state = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
            }
            save_scope_as = financial_center_historic_place
            scope:financial_center_historic_place = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_bond_var_state_1
                    add = root.var:stockpiling_bond_var_2
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

ai_buy_bond_1 = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

    #random_in_global_list = {
    #    variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
    #    save_scope_as = seller
    #}

	random_country = {
		limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes #has bc
			has_financial_center = yes #has fc
			remaining_debt > 0
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75
			not = {
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			}
		}
		save_scope_as = seller
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            scope:buyer.ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_1 = 0
            exists = scope:seller
            scope:seller = {
                not = {
                    this = root
                }
            }
            gold_reserves_var > gold_reserves_10 #reserve sup à 10% de la reserve
			#bond_quantity_scripted >  0
        }

        random_list = {
            1 = { #5Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_1
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

						#seller
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_1
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_1
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_1
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_1
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_1
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_1
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_1
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_1
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_1 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_1
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_1 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_1
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_1
                            multiply = 5
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_1
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_1
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_1
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_1
                            value = 5
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_1_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_1_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_1
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
            1 = { #10Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_1
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_1
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_1
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_1
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_1
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_1
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_1
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_1
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_1 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_1
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_1 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_1
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_1
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_1
                            multiply = 10
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_1
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_1
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_1
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_1
                            value = 10
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_1_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_1_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_1
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
ai_buy_bond_2 = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

    #random_in_global_list = {
    #    variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
    #    save_scope_as = seller
    #}

	random_country = {
		limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes #has bc
			has_financial_center = yes #has fc
			remaining_debt > 0
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75
			not = {
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			}
		}
		save_scope_as = seller
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            scope:buyer.ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_2 = 0
            exists = scope:seller
            scope:seller = {
                not = {
                    this = root
                }
            }
            gold_reserves_var > gold_reserves_10 #reserve sup à 10% de la reserve
			#bond_quantity_scripted >  0
        }

        random_list = {
            1 = { #5Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_2
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_2
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

						#seller
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_2
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_2
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_2
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_2
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_2
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_2
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_2
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_2
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_2 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_2
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_2 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_2
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_2
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_2
                            multiply = 5
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_2
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_2
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_2
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_2
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_2
                            value = 5
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_2_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_2_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_2
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
            1 = { #10Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_2
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_2
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_2
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_2
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_2
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_2
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_2
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_2
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_2
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_2 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_2
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_2 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_2
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_2
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_2
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_2
                            multiply = 10
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_2
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_2
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_2
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_2
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_2
                            value = 10
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_2_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_2_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_2
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_4_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_4
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
ai_buy_bond_5 = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

    #random_in_global_list = {
    #    variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
    #    save_scope_as = seller
    #}

	random_country = {
		limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes #has bc
			has_financial_center = yes #has fc
			remaining_debt > 0
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75
			not = {
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			}
		}
		save_scope_as = seller
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            scope:buyer.ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_5 = 0
            exists = scope:seller
            scope:seller = {
                not = {
                    this = root
                }
            }
            gold_reserves_var > gold_reserves_10 #reserve sup à 10% de la reserve
			#bond_quantity_scripted >  0
        }

        random_list = {
            1 = { #5Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_5
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_5
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

						#seller
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_5
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_5
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_5
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_5
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_5
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_5
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_5
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_5
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_5 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_5
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_5 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_5
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_5
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_5
                            multiply = 5
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_5
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_5
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_5
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_5
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_5
                            value = 5
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_5_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_5_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_5
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
            1 = { #10Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_5
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_5
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_5
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_5
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_5
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_5
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_5
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_5
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_5
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_5 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_5
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_5 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_5
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_5
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_5
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_5
                            multiply = 10
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_5
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_5
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_5
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_5
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_5
                            value = 10
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_5_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_5_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_5
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_7
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
ai_buy_bond_8 = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

    #random_in_global_list = {
    #    variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
    #    save_scope_as = seller
    #}

	random_country = {
		limit = {
			has_central_bank_SS_BS_GS_GES_NISO = yes #has bc
			has_financial_center = yes #has fc
			remaining_debt > 0
			market_owner_is_root_4 = yes
			central_bank_metal_reserves_state_to_ensure_the_conversion_pourcent < 0.75
			not = {
				has_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			}
		}
		save_scope_as = seller
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            scope:buyer.ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_8 = 0
            exists = scope:seller
            scope:seller = {
                not = {
                    this = root
                }
            }
            gold_reserves_var > gold_reserves_10 #reserve sup à 10% de la reserve
			#bond_quantity_scripted >  0
        }

        random_list = {
            1 = { #5Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_8
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_8
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

						#seller
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_8
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_8
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_8
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_8
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_8
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_8
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_8
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_8
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_8 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_8
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_8 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_5Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_8
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_8
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_8
                            multiply = 5
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_8
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_8
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_8
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_8
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_8
                            value = 5
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_8_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_8_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_8
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
            1 = { #10Years
                scope:seller = {
                    scope:buyer = {
                        # Pour les liste du vendeur
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_buyer_country_8
                            target = prev
                        }
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_8
                            target = scope:seller #prev
                        }

                       #seller save scope
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_seller_country_general_8
                            value = scope:seller
                        }

                        ######
                        #quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_bond_quantity_8
                            value = bond_quantity_scripted
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_quantity_purchasing_8
                            value = var:ai_bond_quantity_8
                        }

                        #interret lors de l'achat
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_purchasing_8
                            value = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #valeur de la quantité
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_8
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_8
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_8 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_total_bond_value_8
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }

                        #interet total
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            value = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            multiply = var:ai_bond_quantity_8 #bond quantité
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            multiply = scope:seller.bond_price
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_calculated_8
                            multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
                        }

                        #interet total à terme
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_8
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_8
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_8
                            multiply = 10
                        }

                        #interet par mois
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_8
                            value = var:ai_interest_calculated_8
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_8
                            divide = 12
                        }

                        add_treasury = {
                            subtract = var:ai_total_bond_value_8
                        }

                        interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes

                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_maturity_time_8
                            value = 10
                        }

                        #demare le on_action
                        set_variable = {
                            name = ai_buy_bond_8_on
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #notification
                    every_country = {
                        limit  = {
                            is_player = yes
                        }
                        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
                        }
                        scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                            post_notification = ai_selle_bond_maturity_8_message
                        }
                    }

                    #################
                    #ajout à la liste des acheteur
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list_8
                        target = scope:buyer
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

    }

#_1
ai_privat_bank_bond_1 = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

	random_in_global_list = {
		variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
		save_scope_as = seller
	}


	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
	}

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
	}
	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
	}
	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
	}

	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
	}
	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11

	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_1
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_1
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_1
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_1 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_1
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_1
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_1_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_1_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_1 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}
