		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_3
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_3
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_3
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_3
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_3
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_3 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_3
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_3
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_3
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_3
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_3
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_3_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_3_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_3 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_5
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_5
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_5
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_5
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_5_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_5_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_5 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_6
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_6
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_6
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_6 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_6
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_6
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_6_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_6_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_6 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }

		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
	}

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
	}
	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_8
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_8
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_8
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_8
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_8
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_8 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_8
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_8
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_8
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_8
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_8
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_8_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_8_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_8 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_10
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_10
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_10
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_10
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_10
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_10 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_10
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_10
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_10
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_10
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_10
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_10_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_10_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_10 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_13
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_13
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_13
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_13 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_13
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_13
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_13_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_13_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_13 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_15
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_15
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_15
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_15
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_15
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_15 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_15
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_15
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_15
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_15
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_15
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_15_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_15_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_15 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

		}
    }
}
#_18
ai_privat_bank_bond_18 = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

	random_in_global_list = {
		variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
		save_scope_as = seller
	}


	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
	}
	random_in_list = {

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22

		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23

		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_18
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_18
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_18
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_18
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_18
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_18 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_18
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_18
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_18
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_18
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_18
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_18_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_18_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_18 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_20
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_20
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_20
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_20
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_20
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_20 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_20
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_20
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_20
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_20
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_20
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_20_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_20_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_20 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_22
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_22
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_22_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_22_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_22 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_23
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_23
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_23
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_23
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_23
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_23 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_23
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_23
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_23
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_23
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_23
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_23_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_23_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_23 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
	}
	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		save_scope_as = scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller
			not = {
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_2
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_3
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_4
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_7
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_8
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_9
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_10
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_11
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_14
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_15
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_16
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_17
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_20
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_21
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_22
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_23
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_24
				scope:seller = scope:scope_ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
			}
        }
		scope:seller = {
			scope:buyer = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_25
					value = 1 #slot pris
				}

				#selection de la bank
				random_in_list = {
					variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}

				# Pour les liste du vendeur
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_25
					target = scope:buyer_privat_bank #prev
				}
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
					target = scope:seller #prev
				}

				######
				#quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_25
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
					multiply = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_25 #bond quantité
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}

				#interet total
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_25
					value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_25
					multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
				}
			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_selle_bond_maturity_25_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_buy_bond_maturity_25_message
				}
			}

			#central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes

			#################
			#ajout à la liste des acheteur
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_25 #plusieur bank peuvent etre stack dans cette liste
				target = scope:buyer_privat_bank
			}
		}
    }
}


#_1 -> à modifier car doit aussi comprendre un netoyage des varriable si uz bank disparée
ai_privat_bank_bond_1_renforcement = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
		save_scope_as = seller_1
	}

	#renforcement
    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller_1
			scope:seller_1.remaining_debt > 0
        }
		scope:seller_1 = {
			scope:buyer = {
				random_in_list = {
					variable = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_1
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_1
					add = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1_new
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1_new
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
					add = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1_new
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1_new > 0
					}
					#interet total -> recalcule total
					set_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_1
						value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_1
						multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
					}
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1_new
				}
 			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_selle_bond_maturity_1_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_1_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_1
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_1
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_1

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_1
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_1
    }
}

					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_5_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_5
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_5
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_5
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_5
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_5
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_5

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_5
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_5
    }
}
#_6 -> à modifier car doit aussi comprendre un netoyage des varriable si uz bank disparée
ai_privat_bank_bond_6_renforcement = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
		save_scope_as = seller_6
	}

	#renforcement
    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller_6
			scope:seller_6.remaining_debt > 0
        }
		scope:seller_6 = {
			scope:buyer = {
				random_in_list = {
					variable = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_6
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_6
					add = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6_new
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6_new
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
					add = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6_new
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6_new > 0
					}
					#interet total -> recalcule total
					set_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_6
						value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_6
						multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
					}
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6_new
				}
 			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_selle_bond_maturity_6_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_6_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_6
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_6
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_6
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_6
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_6
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_6

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_6
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_6
    }
}

					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12_new
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12_new
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12
					add = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12_new
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12_new > 0
					}
					#interet total -> recalcule total
					set_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_12
						value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_12
						multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
					}
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12_new
				}
 			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_selle_bond_maturity_12_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_12_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_12
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_12
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_12
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_12
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_12
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_12

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_12
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_12
    }
}
#_13 -> à modifier car doit aussi comprendre un netoyage des varriable si uz bank disparée
ai_privat_bank_bond_13_renforcement = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
		save_scope_as = seller_13
	}

	#renforcement
    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller_13
			scope:seller_13.remaining_debt > 0
        }
		scope:seller_13 = {
			scope:buyer = {
				random_in_list = {
					variable = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_13
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_13
					add = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13_new
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13_new
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
					add = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13_new
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13_new > 0
					}
					#interet total -> recalcule total
					set_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_13
						value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_13
						multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
					}
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13_new
				}
 			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_selle_bond_maturity_13_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_13_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_13
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_13
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_13
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_13
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_13
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_13

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_13
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_13
    }

		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_18
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_18
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_18
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_18

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_18
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_18
    }
}
#_19 -> à modifier car doit aussi comprendre un netoyage des varriable si uz bank disparée
ai_privat_bank_bond_19_renforcement = {
    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer
    }

	random_in_list = {
		variable = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
		save_scope_as = seller_19
	}

	#renforcement
    if = {
        limit = {
            exists = scope:seller_19
			scope:seller_19.remaining_debt > 0
        }
		scope:seller_19 = {
			scope:buyer = {
				random_in_list = {
					variable = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_19
     			   	save_scope_as = buyer_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_19
					add = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}

				#valeur de la quantité
				set_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19_new
					value = bond_quantity_scripted_privat_bank
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19_new
					multiply = scope:seller.bond_price_in_gold
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19
					add = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19_new
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19_new > 0
					}
					#interet total -> recalcule total
					set_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_19
						value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_19
						multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
					}
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19_new
				}
 			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_selle_bond_maturity_19_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_19_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_19
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_19
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_19
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_19
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_19
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_19

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_19
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_19
    }
}

					#interet total -> recalcule total
					set_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_25
						value = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_25
						multiply = scope:seller.interest_value_10Y
					}
				}
				add_investment_pool = {
					subtract = var:ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25_new
				}
 			}

			#################
			#notification
			every_country = {
				limit  = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:seller = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_selle_bond_maturity_25_message
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:buyer = scope:is_player_for_notification
				}
				scope:is_player_for_notification = {
					post_notification = ai_privat_bank_renforcement_buy_bond_maturity_25_message
				}
			}

			central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = yes
 		}
 	}

	#clear
    if = {
        limit = {
			not = {
				exists = scope:seller_25
			}
        }
		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_buyer_slot_25
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_quantity_25
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_bond_value_25
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_privat_bank_interest_calculated_25
			value = 0
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_buyer_country_25

		clear_variable_list = ai_privat_bank_seller_country_general_25
		clear_variable_list =  central_bank_debt_privat_bank_buyer_list_25
    }
}

				has_company = company_type:company_BankJPMorgan
			}
		}
		add_company = company_type:company_BankJPMorgan

			set_company_state_region = s:STATE_NEW_YORK
		}

			if = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
							level < 10
						}
						not = {
							has_building = building_ef_private_construction
						}
					}
				}
				create_building={
					building="building_ef_private_construction"
					add_ownership={
						company={
							type=company_BankJPMorgan

							levels=10
						}

			NOT = { has_company = company_type:company_PreussischeSeehandlung }
		}

			set_company_state_region = s:STATE_BRANDENBURG
		}

			if = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction level < 10 }
						not = { has_building = building_ef_private_construction }

				}
				create_building = {
					building = "building_ef_private_construction"

							type = company_PreussischeSeehandlung
							country = "c:GER"
							levels = 10
						}

		add_company = company_type:company_BankOfBombay	
		company:company_BankOfBombay = {
			set_company_state_region = s:STATE_BOMBAY
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction level < 10 }
						not = { has_building = building_ef_private_construction }
					}
				}
				create_building = {
					building = "building_ef_private_construction"
					add_ownership = {
						company = {
							type = company_BankOfBombay
							country = "c:BIC"
							levels = 10
						}
					}
					reserves = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Generic
	###company_private_construction
	if = {
		limit = { 
			maximum_number_companies_exceeded_monthly_pulse >= 1 #les Compagnie classique ne +1 pas comme les bank
			NOT = {
				has_company = company_type:company_private_construction
			} 
			# any_scope_building = { #inutile il possede deja un centre fiancier
			# 	is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
			# 	level >= 1
			# }
		}		
		add_company = company_type:company_private_construction
		random_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = company_private_construction
							level < 10
						}
						not = {
							has_building = company_private_construction
						}
					}
				}
				create_building={
					building="building_ef_private_construction"
					add_ownership={
						company={
							type=company_private_construction
							country="ROOT"
							levels=5
						}
					}
					reserves=1
				}
			}
		}   
	}

bond_maturity_1 = {
	#gui timer
	change_variable = {
		name = selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_1
		add = 1
	}

	#################
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_1 = 4
		}

		every_in_list = {
			variable = seller_country_general_1
			save_scope_as = seller
		}
		post_notification = maturity_arrives_message
	}
	#################

	#maturity
	change_variable = {
		name = selle_bond_maturity_yers_1
		add = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				var:selle_bond_maturity_yers_1 > var:maturity_time_1
				no_longer_exists_1 = 0 #no_longer_exists
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				no_longer_exists_1 = 1
			}
			add_treasury = {
				add = var:total_bond_value_1
			}
		}

		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = buy_bond_1_on
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = interest_purchasing_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = bond_quantity_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = quantity_purchasing_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = interest_calculated_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = total_bond_value_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = interest_at_term_calculated_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = interest_per_month_calculated_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = selle_bond_maturity_yers_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = seller_country_general_1
			value = 0
		}

		#seller
		every_in_list = {
			variable = seller_country_general_1
			central_bank_debt_buyer_list_1_clear = yes
			#save_scope_as = seller
		}

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = buyer_country_1
		clear_variable_list = seller_country_1

		clear_variable_list = seller_country_general_1
		clear_variable_list = seller_country_general_in_currency_1
		clear_variable_list = buyer_country_general_1

		interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes
	}
}

ai_bond_maturity_1 = {
	#gui timer
	change_variable = {
		name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_1
		add = 1
	}
	#maturity
	change_variable = {
		name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_1
		add = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {

		# scope:seller = {
		# 	central_bank_debt_buyer_list_9_clear = yes
		# }

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_buyer_country_9
		clear_variable_list = ai_seller_country_9

		clear_variable_list = ai_seller_country_general_9
		clear_variable_list = ai_buyer_country_general_9
		interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes
	}
}
ai_bond_maturity_10 = {
	#gui timer
	change_variable = {
		name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_10
		add = 1
	}
	#maturity
	change_variable = {
		name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_10
		add = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				var:ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_10 = var:ai_maturity_time_10
				ai_no_longer_exists_10 = 0 #no_longer_exists
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ai_no_longer_exists_10 = 1
			}
			add_treasury = {
				add = var:ai_total_bond_value_10
			}
		}

		#Reset variable
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_buy_bond_10_on
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_interest_purchasing_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_bond_quantity_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_quantity_purchasing_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_time_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_interest_calculated_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_total_bond_value_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_interest_at_term_calculated_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_interest_per_month_calculated_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_yers_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_selle_bond_maturity_on_action_10
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ai_seller_country_general_10
			value = 0
		}

		#seller
		every_in_list = {
			variable = ai_seller_country_general_10
			central_bank_debt_buyer_list_10_clear = yes
			#save_scope_as = seller
		}
		# scope:seller = {
		# 	central_bank_debt_buyer_list_10_clear = yes
		# }

		#Reset list
		clear_variable_list = ai_buyer_country_10
		clear_variable_list = ai_seller_country_10

		clear_variable_list = ai_seller_country_general_10
		clear_variable_list = ai_buyer_country_general_10
		interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes
	}
}

central_bank_interest_refund_per_year_in_gold = {

	#gold_loaned_to_central_bank reset gold_loaned_to_central_bank
	if = {
		limit = {
			gold_loaned_to_central_bank >= 0
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_historic
			subtract = central_bank_interest_refund_per_year
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_historic
			multiply = 0.8
		}
	}

	############
	#reset gold_loaned_to_central_bank_historic
	############
	if = {
		limit = {
			gold_loaned_to_central_bank < 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_historic #gold_loaned_to_central_bank_historic
			value = 0
		}
	}

	############
	#fixe var
	############
	#gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
	set_variable = {
		name = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix
		value = gold_loaned_to_central_bank
	}

	#gui -> gold_loaned_to_central_bank_no_interest_fix
	set_variable = {
		name = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_no_interest_fix #-> [Country.MakeScope.Var('gold_loaned_to_central_bank_no_interest_fix').GetValue|D+]
		value = gold_loaned_to_central_bank_no_interest
	}
}
interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = {
	remove_modifier = interest_from_foreign_debt_investment
	add_modifier = {
		name = interest_from_foreign_debt_investment
		multiplier = interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment
	}
}

		#building_food_industry
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_food_industry

					private_ownership_fraction > 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_food_industry
					production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
				}

			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_food_industry
				production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_building = building_food_industry

					private_ownership_fraction <= 0.5
				}

					production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock

				building_type = building_food_industry
				production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
			}
		}

fluctuations_country_indice_value_year = {
	change_variable = {
		name = index_value_count
		add = 1
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            var:index_value_count = 1
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_1
            value = country_indice
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            var:index_value_count = 2
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_2
            value = country_indice
        }

        set_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            value = 0
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            add = var:country_indice_value_2
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            subtract = var:country_indice_value_1
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            divide = var:country_indice_value_1
        }

		#change base_index_value
		set_variable = {
			name = base_index_value_dif
			value = var:base_index_value
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = base_index_value_dif
			multiply = var:country_indice_value_dif_01
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					var:base_index_value < 1000000 #point
					base_index_value_dif < 0
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = base_index_value
				add = var:base_index_value_dif
			}
		}

        set_variable = {
            name = index_value_count
            value = 0
        }

		if = {
			limit = {
				var:country_indice_value_dif_01 < -0.5
			}
			financial_crash = yes
		}
    }
}
fluctuations_country_indice_value_year_clear = {
	set_variable = {
		name = country_indice_value_dif_01
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = base_index_value_dif
		value = 0
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {

		}
	}

	scope:seller = {
		if = {
			limit = {
