currency_crisis = {
	#objectif:
	# - la devise baisse de 50% -> les pays étranger perde la confiance -> revente massive de la devise -> inflation scripter qui calcule la différence excte de valeur etre les 2 extreme de valeur
	# - revente integrale de la devise possedé par les pays étranger
	# - control des change pour ne pas etre acheter
	# - blocage des route de commerce

	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = currency_crisis
		value = 1
	}
	currency_crisis_count_reset = yes
	country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
			or = {
				is_at_war = yes
				var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				has_interest_marker_in_region = root.capital.region
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.1
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
}
economic_crisis = {
	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = economic_crisis
		value = 1
	}
	economic_crisis_count_reset = yes
	#country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			#is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			global_country_ranking < 100  #all pays
			#has_modifier = has_central_bank
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
			or = {
				is_at_war = yes
				var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				has_interest_marker_in_region = root.capital.region
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.2
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
} #-> revante devise en mass + pas de rachat si foreign_exchange_controls
financial_crash = {
	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = financial_crash
		value = 1
	}
	financial_crash_count_reset = yes
	#country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			has_modifier = has_financial_center
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
			or = {
				is_at_war = yes
				var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				has_interest_marker_in_region = root.capital.region
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.3
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
}
central_bank_bankruptcy = {
	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	if = {
		limit  = {
			or = {
				var:economic_instability_count = 0
				var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 0
			}  
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = money_value_target_1
			divide = 2
		}
		trade_balance = yes #j'actualisa la trade balance direct car des le mois suivant le central_bank_bankruptcy va retrigger si le pats est toujour en extreme weak
	}

	set_variable = {
		name = central_bank_bankruptcy
		value = 1
	}
	central_bank_bankruptcy_count_reset = yes
	#country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			not = {
				has_modifier = economic_instability
			}
			# or = {
			# 	is_at_war = yes
			# 	var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			# }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				has_interest_marker_in_region = root.capital.region
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.4
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
} #-> revante devise en mass + pas de rachat si foreign_exchange_controls
country_bankruptcy = {
	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = country_bankruptcy
		value = 1
	}

	#country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			global_country_ranking < 50 #all pays
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				has_interest_marker_in_region = root.capital.region
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.5
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
}
########################################################################################

economic_instability = {

	########################################################################################
	# #test
	# set_variable = {
	# 	name = country_indice_value_dif_01
	# 	value = -0.6
	# }
	########################################################################################

	root = {
		save_scope_as = target_country
	}
	#Country Bankrupt - ok

	#event: ? si déclanche grace au trigger

	#Bank central Bankrupt = weak currency - ok
	#Crise monetaire = currency crisis (diminution de la valeur de la devise de plus de 50%/) -> délock l'inflation -> création d'inflation dans le monetary policy -> crise inflationniste du a la dette à vopitr
	#Crise économique =  Economic crisis (diminution de la valeur du PIB de plus de 50%)
	#Crash financier = Financial crash (diminution de la valeur de l'index des marché de plus de 50%)

		#pour le modifier economic_instability les pays sont vendeur sur la devise meme en dehor d'une crise de la dvise


	##############
	#General
	##############

	#perte de prestige 25% voir plus
	#malus diplomatique avec tout les pays uniquement si default sur dette

	##############
	#evenement spe
	##############

	change_variable = {
		name = economic_instability_count
		add = 1
	}
	economic_instability_count_reset = yes

	#economic_instability notif
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count = 1
		}
		every_country = { #notif for player
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				has_interest_marker_in_region = root.capital.region

				root = {
					not = {
						or  = {
							is_at_war = yes
							is_revolutionary = yes
							#var:country_bankruptcy = 1
							market_owner_is_root_univ_with_buiding = yes
							is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.6
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}

	#economic_instability concequences
	if = {
		limit  = {
			or  = {
				var:economic_instability_count >= 2
				var:country_bankruptcy >= 1
				#is_at_war = yes #idée que si tu est en guerre alors tu trigger des le premier avertissement
				#var:central_bank_bankruptcy >= 1 #-> Teste division pa 2 de la money value target pour essayer de sauvé le pays avant de déclanché la crise
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:economic_instability_count = 1 #en cas de country_bankruptcy ou de central_bank_bankruptcy l'évenement economic_instability ce déclanche meme si l'instabilité est que de 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = economic_instability_count
				value = 2 #cela bloque l'attribution de note
			}
		}

		#country_bankruptcy
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:country_bankruptcy >= 1
				not = {
					has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
				}
			}

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_C
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability
				months = 23
			}

			# remove_modifier = modifierr vanila
			# add_modifier = {
			# 	name = modifierr vanila
			# 	months = 23
			# }
		}

		# currency_crisis/central_bank_bankruptcy
		if = {
			limit  = {
				or = {
					var:currency_crisis >= 1
					var:central_bank_bankruptcy >= 1
				}
				not = {
					or = {
						has_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
						has_modifier = currency_crisis_country
					}
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
			add_modifier = {
				name = foreign_exchange_controls
				months = 23
			}

			#déplacé dans le currency_strength_modifier pour etre sure de déétruire la masse monetaire dans la balance si jamais
			#mais je le laisse ici pour le currency_crisis
			if = {
				limit  = {
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					not = {
						has_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					if = {
						limit  = {
							has_modifier = has_central_bank
							not = {
								this = root
								#is_subject = yes #à voir car  il faut  que  tout  soit  vendu
							}
						}
						save_scope_as = seller
						all_currency_resold = yes
					}
				}
			}

			#-> création d'hyper inflation scripté

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_D
				months = 23
				#-> blocage des route de commerce qui devrai rester grace au extreme weak currency (pas besoins d'un modificateur siupplémentaire)
				#-> nécessité d'atribué le extrem weak currency oui ou non ? -> deja présent pour la bank central bankrupcy car c'est le ex xeak qui le déclanche
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability
				months = 23
			}
			if = {
				limit  = {
					var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				}
				remove_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
				add_modifier = {
					name = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
					months = 23
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit  = {
					var:currency_crisis = 1
				}
				remove_modifier = currency_crisis_country
				add_modifier = {
					name = currency_crisis_country
					months = 23
				}
			}

			#passage en fiat currency car plus d'import possible d'or ou d'argznt
			activate_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard
			central_bank_production_methods = yes
		}

		#financial_crash
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:financial_crash >= 1
				not = {
					has_modifier = financial_crash_country
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit  = {
					# not = {
					# 	is_subject = yes
					# }
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					has_modifier = has_financial_center
				}
				financial_crash_consequences = yes
			}

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_CC
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability #bloc l'achat de  la devise et favorrise sa vente / bloc le base ratre à 10%
				months = 23
			}
			remove_modifier = financial_crash_country
			add_modifier = {
				name = financial_crash_country
				multiplier = var:country_indice_value_dif_01
				months = 23
			}
		}

		#economic_crisis
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:economic_crisis >= 1
				not = {
					has_modifier = economic_crisis_country
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit  = {
					# not = {
					# 	is_subject = yes
					# }
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					has_modifier = has_financial_center
				}
				economic_crisis_consequences = yes
			}

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_C
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability #bloc l'achat de  la devise et favorrise sa vente / bloc le base ratre à 10%
				months = 23
			}
			remove_modifier = economic_crisis_country
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_crisis_country
				months = 23
			}
		}

		country_credit_rating = yes
	}
}

########################################################################################

bankrupt_company = {
    if = {
		limit = {
			has_company = company_type:company_basic_agriculture_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				company:company_basic_agriculture_1.prosperity < 100
			}
			remove_company = company_type:company_basic_agriculture_1
		}
	}
    if = {
		limit = {
			has_company = company_type:company_basic_agriculture_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				company:company_basic_agriculture_2.prosperity < 100
			}
			remove_company = company_type:company_basic_agriculture_2
		}
	}
    if = {
		limit = {
			has_company = company_type:company_basic_fabrics
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				company:company_basic_fabrics.prosperity < 100
			}
			remove_company = company_type:company_basic_fabrics
		}
	}
    if = {
		limit = {
			has_company = company_type:company_basic_colonial_plantations_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				company:company_basic_colonial_plantations_1.prosperity < 100
			}
			remove_company = company_type:company_basic_colonial_plantations_1
		}
	}
    if = {
		limit = {
			has_company = company_type:company_basic_colonial_plantations_2
		}
		if = {
